DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('/*')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('*')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('$(D std._parallelism) implements high-level primitives for SMP _parallelism.')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('These include parallel foreach, parallel reduce, parallel eager map, pipelining')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('and future')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('/')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('promise _parallelism.  $(D std._parallelism) is recommended when the')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('same operation is to be executed in parallel on different data, or when a')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('function is to be executed in a background thread and its result returned to a')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('well-defined main thread.  For communication between arbitrary threads, see')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('$(D std.concurrency).')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('$(D std._parallelism) is based on the concept of a $(D Task).  A $(D Task) is an')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('object that represents the fundamental unit of work in this library and may be')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('executed in parallel with any other $(D Task).  Using $(D Task)')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('directly allows programming with a future')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('/')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('promise paradigm.  All other')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('supported _parallelism paradigms (parallel foreach, map, reduce, pipelining)')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('represent an additional level of abstraction over $(D Task).  They')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('automatically create one or more $(D Task) objects, or closely related types')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('that are conceptually identical but not part of the public API.')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('After creation, a $(D Task) may be executed in a new thread, or submitted')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('to a $(D TaskPool) for execution.  A $(D TaskPool) encapsulates a task queue')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('and its worker threads.  Its purpose is to efficiently map a large')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('number of $(D Task)s onto a smaller number of threads.  A task queue is a')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('FIFO queue of $(D Task) objects that have been submitted to the')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('$(D TaskPool) and are awaiting execution.  A worker thread is a thread that')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('is associated with exactly one task queue.  It executes the $(D Task) at the')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('front of its queue when the queue has work available, or sleeps when')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('no work is available.  Each task queue is associated with zero or')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('more worker threads.  If the result of a $(D Task) is needed before execution')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('by a worker thread has begun, the $(D Task) can be removed from the task queue')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('and executed immediately in the thread where the result is needed.')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('Warning:  Unless marked as $(D @trusted) or $(D @safe), artifacts in')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('          this module allow implicit data sharing between threads and cannot')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('          guarantee that client code is free from low level data races.')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('Source:    $(PHOBOSSRC std')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('/')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('_parallelism.d)')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('Author:  David Simcha')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('Copyright:  Copyright (c) 2009-2011, David Simcha.')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('License:    $(HTTP boost.org')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('/')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('LICENSE_1_0.txt, Boost License 1.0)')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('*/')

DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('value, if any.  These functions and $(D done) also act as full memory barriers,')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')

DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('/*')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('*')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('Creates a $(D Task) on the GC heap that calls an alias.  This may be executed')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('via $(D Task.executeInNewThread) or by submitting to a')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('$(REF TaskPool, std,parallelism).  A globally accessible instance of')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('$(D TaskPool) is provided by $(REF taskPool, std,parallelism).')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('Returns:  A pointer to the $(D Task).')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('Example:')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('---')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('//')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT (' Read two files into memory at the same time.')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('import std.file;')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('void main()')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('{')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    ')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('//')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT (' Create and execute a Task for reading')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    ')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('//')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT (' foo.txt.')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    auto file1Task = task!read("foo.txt");')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    file1Task.executeInNewThread();')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    ')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('//')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT (' Read bar.txt in parallel.')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    auto file2Data = read("bar.txt");')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    ')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('//')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT (' Get the results of reading foo.txt.')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    auto file1Data = file1Task.yieldForce;')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('}')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('---')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('---')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('//')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT (' Sorts an array using a parallel quick sort algorithm.')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('//')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT (' The first partition is done serially.  Both recursion')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('//')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT (' branches are then executed in parallel.')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('//')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('//')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT (' Timings for sorting an array of 1,000,000 doubles on')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('//')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT (' an Athlon 64 X2 dual core machine:')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('//')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('//')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT (' This implementation:               176 milliseconds.')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('//')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT (' Equivalent serial implementation:  280 milliseconds')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('void parallelSort(T)(T[] data)')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('{')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    ')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('//')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT (' Sort small subarrays serially.')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    if (data.length < 100)')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    {')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('         std.algorithm.sort(data);')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('         return;')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    }')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    ')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('//')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT (' Partition the array.')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    swap(data[$ ')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('/')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT (' 2], data[$ - 1]);')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    auto pivot = data[$ - 1];')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    bool lessThanPivot(T elem) { return elem < pivot; }')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    auto greaterEqual = partition!lessThanPivot(data[0..$ - 1]);')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    swap(data[$ - greaterEqual.length - 1], data[$ - 1]);')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    auto less = data[0..$ - greaterEqual.length - 1];')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    greaterEqual = data[$ - greaterEqual.length..$];')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    ')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('//')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT (' Execute both recursion branches in parallel.')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    auto recurseTask = task!parallelSort(greaterEqual);')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    taskPool.put(recurseTask);')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    parallelSort(less);')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    recurseTask.yieldForce;')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('}')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('---')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('*/')

DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('/*')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('*')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('This class encapsulates a task queue and a set of worker threads.  Its purpose')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('is to efficiently map a large number of $(D Task)s onto a smaller number of')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('threads.  A task queue is a FIFO queue of $(D Task) objects that have been')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('submitted to the $(D TaskPool) and are awaiting execution.  A worker thread is a')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('thread that executes the $(D Task) at the front of the queue when one is')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('available and sleeps when the queue is empty.')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('This class should usually be used via the global instantiation')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('available via the $(REF taskPool, std,parallelism) property.')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('Occasionally it is useful to explicitly instantiate a $(D TaskPool):')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('1.  When you want $(D TaskPool) instances with multiple priorities, for example')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    a low priority pool and a high priority pool.')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('2.  When the threads in the global task pool are waiting on a synchronization')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    primitive (for example a mutex), and you want to parallelize the code that')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    needs to run before these threads can be resumed.')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT (' ')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('*/')

WHITE_SPACE ('    ')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('/*')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('*')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    Implements a parallel foreach loop over a range.  This works by implicitly')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    creating and submitting one $(D Task) to the $(D TaskPool) for each worker')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    thread.  A work unit is a set of consecutive elements of $(D range) to')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    be processed by a worker thread between communication with any other')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    thread.  The number of elements processed per work unit is controlled by the')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    $(D workUnitSize) parameter.  Smaller work units provide better load')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    balancing, but larger work units avoid the overhead of communicating')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    with other threads frequently to fetch the next work unit.  Large work')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    units also avoid false sharing in cases where the range is being modified.')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    The less time a single iteration of the loop takes, the larger')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    $(D workUnitSize) should be.  For very expensive loop bodies,')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    $(D workUnitSize) should  be 1.  An overload that chooses a default work')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    unit size is also available.')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    Example:')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    ---')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    ')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('//')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT (' Find the logarithm of every number from 1 to')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    ')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('//')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT (' 10_000_000 in parallel.')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    auto logs = new double[10_000_000];')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    ')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('//')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT (' Parallel foreach works with or without an index')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    ')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('//')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT (' variable.  It can be iterate by ref if range.front')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    ')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('//')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT (' returns by ref.')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    ')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('//')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT (' Iterate over logs using work units of size 100.')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    foreach (i, ref elem; taskPool.parallel(logs, 100))')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    {')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        elem = log(i + 1.0);')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    }')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    ')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('//')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT (' Same thing, but use the default work unit size.')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    ')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('//')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    ')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('//')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT (' Timings on an Athlon 64 X2 dual core machine:')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    ')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('//')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    ')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('//')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT (' Parallel foreach:  388 milliseconds')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    ')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('//')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT (' Regular foreach:   619 milliseconds')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    foreach (i, ref elem; taskPool.parallel(logs))')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    {')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        elem = log(i + 1.0);')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    }')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    ---')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    Notes:')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    The memory usage of this implementation is guaranteed to be constant')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    in $(D range.length).')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    Breaking from a parallel foreach loop via a break, labeled break,')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    labeled continue, return or goto statement throws a')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    $(D ParallelForeachError).')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    In the case of non-random access ranges, parallel foreach buffers lazily')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    to an array of size $(D workUnitSize) before executing the parallel portion')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    of the loop.  The exception is that, if a parallel foreach is executed')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    over a range returned by $(D asyncBuf) or $(D map), the copying is elided')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    and the buffers are simply swapped.  In this case $(D workUnitSize) is')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    ignored and the work unit size is set to the  buffer size of $(D range).')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    A memory barrier is guaranteed to be executed on exit from the loop,')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    so that results produced by all threads are visible in the calling thread.')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    $(B Exception Handling):')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    When at least one exception is thrown from inside a parallel foreach loop,')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    the submission of additional $(D Task) objects is terminated as soon as')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    possible, in a non-deterministic manner.  All executing or')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    enqueued work units are allowed to complete.  Then, all exceptions that')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    were thrown by any work unit are chained using $(D Throwable.next) and')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    rethrown.  The order of the exception chaining is non-deterministic.')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    ')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('*/')

DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('/*')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('*')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        Eager parallel map.  The eagerness of this function means it has less')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        overhead than the lazily evaluated $(D TaskPool.map) and should be')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        preferred where the memory requirements of eagerness are acceptable.')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        $(D functions) are the functions to be evaluated, passed as template')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        alias parameters in a style similar to')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        $(REF map, std,algorithm,iteration).')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        The first argument must be a random access range. For performance')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        reasons, amap will assume the range elements have not yet been')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        initialized. Elements will be overwritten without calling a destructor')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        nor doing an assignment. As such, the range must not contain meaningful')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        data: either un-initialized objects, or objects in their $(D .init)')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        state.')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        ---')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        auto numbers = iota(100_000_000.0);')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        ')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('//')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT (' Find the square roots of numbers.')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        ')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('//')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        ')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('//')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT (' Timings on an Athlon 64 X2 dual core machine:')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        ')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('//')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        ')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('//')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT (' Parallel eager map:                   0.802 s')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        ')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('//')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT (' Equivalent serial implementation:     1.768 s')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        auto squareRoots = taskPool.amap!sqrt(numbers);')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        ---')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        Immediately after the range argument, an optional work unit size argument')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        may be provided.  Work units as used by $(D amap) are identical to those')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        defined for parallel foreach.  If no work unit size is provided, the')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        default work unit size is used.')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        ---')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        ')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('//')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT (' Same thing, but make work unit size 100.')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        auto squareRoots = taskPool.amap!sqrt(numbers, 100);')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        ---')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        An output range for returning the results may be provided as the last')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        argument.  If one is not provided, an array of the proper type will be')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        allocated on the garbage collected heap.  If one is provided, it must be a')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        random access range with assignable elements, must have reference')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        semantics with respect to assignment to its elements, and must have the')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        same length as the input range.  Writing to adjacent elements from')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        different threads must be safe.')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        ---')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        ')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('//')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT (' Same thing, but explicitly allocate an array')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        ')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('//')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT (' to return the results in.  The element type')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        ')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('//')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT (' of the array may be either the exact type')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        ')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('//')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT (' returned by functions or an implicit conversion')

DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        ')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('//')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT (' target.')

DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        auto squareRoots = new float[numbers.length];')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        taskPool.amap!sqrt(numbers, squareRoots);')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        ')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('//')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT (' Multiple functions, explicit output range, and')

DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        ')

DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        ---')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        Note:')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        A memory barrier is guaranteed to be executed after all results are written')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        but before returning so that results produced by all threads are visible')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        in the calling thread.')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        Tips:')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')

DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        input and output range.')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')

DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')

DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        $(B Exception Handling):')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        When at least one exception is thrown from inside the map functions,')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        the submission of additional $(D Task) objects is terminated as soon as')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        possible, in a non-deterministic manner.  All currently executing or')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        enqueued work units are allowed to complete.  Then, all exceptions that')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        were thrown from any work unit are chained using $(D Throwable.next) and')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        rethrown.  The order of the exception chaining is non-deterministic.')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        ')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('*/')

DlangTokenType.{ ('{')
WHITE_SPACE ('\n')
WHITE_SPACE ('        ')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('/*')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('*')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        A semi-lazy parallel map that can be used for pipelining.  The map')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        functions are evaluated for the first $(D bufSize) elements and stored in a')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        buffer and made available to $(D popFront).  Meanwhile, in the')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        background a second buffer of the same size is filled.  When the first')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        buffer is exhausted, it is swapped with the second buffer and filled while')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        the values from what was originally the second buffer are read.  This')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        implementation allows for elements to be written to the buffer without')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        the need for atomic operations or synchronization for each write, and')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        enables the mapping function to be evaluated efficiently in parallel.')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        $(D map) has more overhead than the simpler procedure used by $(D amap)')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        but avoids the need to keep all results in memory simultaneously and works')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        with non-random access ranges.')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        Params:')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        source = The input range to be mapped.  If $(D source) is not random')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        access it will be lazily buffered to an array of size $(D bufSize) before')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        the map function is evaluated.  (For an exception to this rule, see Notes.)')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        bufSize = The size of the buffer to store the evaluated elements.')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        workUnitSize = The number of elements to evaluate in a single')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        $(D Task).  Must be less than or equal to $(D bufSize), and')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        should be a fraction of $(D bufSize) such that all worker threads can be')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        used.  If the default of size_t.max is used, workUnitSize will be set to')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        the pool-wide default.')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        Returns:  An input range representing the results of the map.  This range')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('                  has a length iff $(D source) has a length.')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        Notes:')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        If a range returned by $(D map) or $(D asyncBuf) is used as an input to')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        $(D map), then as an optimization the copying from the output buffer')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        of the first range to the input buffer of the second range is elided, even')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        though the ranges returned by $(D map) and $(D asyncBuf) are non-random')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        access ranges.  This means that the $(D bufSize) parameter passed to the')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        current call to $(D map) will be ignored and the size of the buffer')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        will be the buffer size of $(D source).')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        Example:')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        ---')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        ')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('//')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT (' Pipeline reading a file, converting each line')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        ')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('//')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT (' to a number, taking the logarithms of the numbers,')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        ')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('//')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT (' and performing the additions necessary to find')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        ')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('//')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT (' the sum of the logarithms.')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        auto lineRange = File("numberList.txt").byLine();')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        auto dupedLines = std.algorithm.map!"a.idup"(lineRange);')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        auto nums = taskPool.map!(to!double)(dupedLines);')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        auto logs = taskPool.map!log10(nums);')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        double sum = 0;')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        foreach (elem; logs)')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        {')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('            sum += elem;')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        }')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        ---')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        $(B Exception Handling):')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        Any exceptions thrown while iterating over $(D source)')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        or computing the map function are re-thrown on a call to $(D popFront) or,')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        if thrown during construction, are simply allowed to propagate to the')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        caller.  In the case of exceptions thrown while computing the map function,')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        the exceptions are chained as in $(D TaskPool.amap).')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        ')

DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    Given a $(D source) range that is expensive to iterate over, returns an')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    input range that asynchronously buffers the contents of')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    $(D source) into a buffer of $(D bufSize) elements in a worker thread,')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    while making previously buffered elements from a second buffer, also of size')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    $(D bufSize), available via the range interface of the returned')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    object.  The returned range has a length iff $(D hasLength!S).')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    $(D asyncBuf) is useful, for example, when performing expensive operations')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    on the elements of ranges that represent data on a disk or network.')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    Example:')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')

DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        ')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('//')

DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        ')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('//')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT (' Fetch more lines in the background while we')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        ')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('//')

DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        ')

WHITE_SPACE ('    ')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('/*')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('*')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    Given a callable object $(D next) that writes to a user-provided buffer and')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    a second callable object $(D empty) that determines whether more data is')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    available to write via $(D next), returns an input range that')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    asynchronously calls $(D next) with a set of size $(D nBuffers) of buffers')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    and makes the results available in the order they were obtained via the')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    input range interface of the returned object.  Similarly to the')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    input range overload of $(D asyncBuf), the first half of the buffers')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    are made available via the range interface while the second half are')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    filled and vice-versa.')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    Params:')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    next = A callable object that takes a single argument that must be an array')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('           with mutable elements.  When called, $(D next) writes data to')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('           the array provided by the caller.')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    empty = A callable object that takes no arguments and returns a type')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('            implicitly convertible to $(D bool).  This is used to signify')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('            that no more data is available to be obtained by calling $(D next).')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    initialBufSize = The initial size of each buffer.  If $(D next) takes its')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('                     array by reference, it may resize the buffers.')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    nBuffers = The number of buffers to cycle through when calling $(D next).')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    Example:')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    ---')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    ')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('//')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT (' Fetch lines of a file in a background')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    ')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('//')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT (' thread while processing previously fetched')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    ')

DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')

DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    Warning:')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    Using the range returned by this function in a parallel foreach loop')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    will not work because buffers may be overwritten while the task that')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    processes them is in queue.  This is checked for at compile time')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    and will result in a static assertion failure.')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    ')

WHITE_SPACE ('    ')
DlangTokenType.{ ('{')
WHITE_SPACE ('\n')
WHITE_SPACE ('        ')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('/*')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('*')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        Parallel reduce on a random access range.  Except as otherwise noted,')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        usage is similar to $(REF _reduce, std,algorithm,iteration).  This')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        function works by splitting the range to be reduced into work units,')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        which are slices to be reduced in parallel.  Once the results from all')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        work units are computed, a final serial reduction is performed on these')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        results to compute the final answer. Therefore, care must be taken to')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        choose the seed value appropriately.')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        Because the reduction is being performed in parallel, $(D functions)')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        must be associative.  For notational simplicity, let # be an')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        infix operator representing $(D functions).  Then, (a # b) # c must equal')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        a # (b # c).  Floating point addition is not associative')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        even though addition in exact arithmetic is.  Summing floating')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        point numbers using this function may give different results than summing')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        serially.  However, for many practical purposes floating point addition')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        can be treated as associative.')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        Note that, since $(D functions) are assumed to be associative,')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        additional optimizations are made to the serial portion of the reduction')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        algorithm. These take advantage of the instruction level parallelism of')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        modern CPUs, in addition to the thread-level parallelism that the rest')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        of this module exploits.  This can lead to better than linear speedups')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        relative to $(REF _reduce, std,algorithm,iteration), especially for')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        fine-grained benchmarks like dot products.')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        An explicit seed may be provided as the first argument.  If')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        provided, it is used as the seed for all work units and for the final')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        reduction of results from all work units.  Therefore, if it is not the')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        identity value for the operation being performed, results may differ')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        from those generated by $(REF _reduce, std,algorithm,iteration) or')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        depending on how many work units are used.  The next argument must be')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        the range to be reduced.')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        ---')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        ')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('//')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT (' Find the sum of squares of a range in parallel, using')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        ')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('//')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT (' an explicit seed.')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        ')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('//')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        ')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('//')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT (' Timings on an Athlon 64 X2 dual core machine:')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        ')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('//')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        ')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('//')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT (' Parallel reduce:                     72 milliseconds')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        ')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('//')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT (' Using std.algorithm.reduce instead:  181 milliseconds')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        auto nums = iota(10_000_000.0f);')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        auto sumSquares = taskPool.reduce!"a + b"(')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('            0.0, std.algorithm.map!"a ')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('*')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT (' a"(nums)')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        );')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        ---')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        If no explicit seed is provided, the first element of each work unit')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        is used as a seed.  For the final reduction, the result from the first')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        work unit is used as the seed.')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        ---')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        ')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('//')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT (' Find the sum of a range in parallel, using the first')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        ')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('//')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT (' element of each work unit as the seed.')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        auto sum = taskPool.reduce!"a + b"(nums);')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        ---')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        An explicit work unit size may be specified as the last argument.')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        Specifying too small a work unit size will effectively serialize the')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        reduction, as the final reduction of the result of each work unit will')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        dominate computation time.  If $(D TaskPool.size) for this instance')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        is zero, this parameter is ignored and one work unit is used.')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        ---')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        ')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('//')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT (' Use a work unit size of 100.')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        auto sum2 = taskPool.reduce!"a + b"(nums, 100);')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        ')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('//')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT (' Work unit size of 100 and explicit seed.')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        auto sum3 = taskPool.reduce!"a + b"(0.0, nums, 100);')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        ---')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        Parallel reduce supports multiple functions, like')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        $(D std.algorithm.reduce).')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        ---')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        ')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('//')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT (' Find both the min and max of nums.')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        auto minMax = taskPool.reduce!(min, max)(nums);')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        assert(minMax[0] == reduce!min(nums));')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        assert(minMax[1] == reduce!max(nums));')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        ---')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        $(B Exception Handling):')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        After this function is finished executing, any exceptions thrown')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')

DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        order is non-deterministic.')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('         ')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('*/')

WHITE_SPACE ('    ')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('/*')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('*')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    Struct for creating worker-local storage.  Worker-local storage is')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    thread-local storage that exists only for worker threads in a given')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    $(D TaskPool) plus a single thread outside the pool.  It is allocated on the')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    garbage collected heap in a way that avoids _false sharing, and doesn't')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    necessarily have global scope within any thread.  It can be accessed from')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    any worker thread in the $(D TaskPool) that created it, and one thread')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    outside this $(D TaskPool).  All threads outside the pool that created a')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    given instance of worker-local storage share a single slot.')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    Since the underlying data for this struct is heap-allocated, this struct')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    has reference semantics when passed between functions.')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    The main uses cases for $(D WorkerLocalStorageStorage) are:')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    1.  Performing parallel reductions with an imperative, as opposed to')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    functional, programming style.  In this case, it's useful to treat')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    $(D WorkerLocalStorageStorage) as local to each thread for only the parallel')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    portion of an algorithm.')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    2.  Recycling temporary buffers across iterations of a parallel foreach loop.')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    Example:')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    ---')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    ')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('//')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT (' Calculate pi as in our synopsis example, but')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    ')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('//')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT (' use an imperative instead of a functional style.')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    immutable n = 1_000_000_000;')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    immutable delta = 1.0L ')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('/')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT (' n;')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    auto sums = taskPool.workerLocalStorage(0.0L);')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    foreach (i; parallel(iota(n)))')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('    {')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        immutable x = ( i - 0.5L ) ')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('*')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT (' delta;')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('\n')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('        immutable toAdd = delta ')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('/')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT (' ( 1.0 + x ')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT ('*')
DlangTokenType.BLOCK_COMMENT (' x );')
